<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The controlled <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">HoverCard</code> component provides an interface for managing the state of the hover card using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">open</code> and
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onOpenChange</code> props:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the hover card is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useHoverCard</code> hook. This
way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="delay" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#delay"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Delay</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Control the open and close delay of the hover card using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">openDelay</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">closeDelay</code> props:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="positioning" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#positioning"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Positioning</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">HoverCard</code> component can be customized in its placement and distance from the trigger element through the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">positioning</code> prop:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the hover card&#x27;s state with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">HoverCard.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useHoverCardContext</code> hook:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_59hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_59hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_59hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm <h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">API</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(open: and\n`onOpenChange` props:\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/react/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setOpen(!open)}\u003e\n        Toggle\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Root open={open} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n        \u003cp\u003e\n          Liked by{' '}\n          \u003cHoverCard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} asChild\u003e\n            \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e{' '}\n          and 3 others\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cHoverCard.Arrow className={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n                \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip className={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n              \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.Body}\u003e\n                \u003cimg className={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n                \u003cdiv\u003e\n                  \u003cp className={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                  \u003cp className={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cp className={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/solid/hover-card'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = createSignal(false)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setOpen(!open())}\u003e\n        Toggle\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Root open={open()} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n        \u003cp\u003e\n          Liked by{' '}\n          \u003cHoverCard.Trigger\n            class={styles.Trigger}\n            asChild={(props) =\u003e (\n              \u003ca href=\"#profile\" {...props()}\u003e\n                @sarah_chen\n              \u003c/a\u003e\n            )}\n          /\u003e{' '}\n          and 3 others\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cHoverCard.Arrow class={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n                \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip class={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n              \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n                \u003cimg class={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n                \u003cdiv\u003e\n                  \u003cp class={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                  \u003cp class={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cp class={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/vue/hover-card'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nconst open = ref(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"open = !open\"\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cHoverCard.Root v-model:open=\"open\"\u003e\n      \u003cp\u003e\n        Liked by\n        \u003cHoverCard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" as-child\u003e\n          \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e\n        and 3 others\n      \u003c/p\u003e\n      \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.Arrow :class=\"styles.Arrow\"\u003e\n              \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip :class=\"styles.ArrowTip\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n            \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Body\"\u003e\n              \u003cimg :class=\"styles.Avatar\" src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n              \u003cdiv\u003e\n                \u003cp :class=\"styles.Name\"\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                \u003cp :class=\"styles.Username\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cp :class=\"styles.Bio\"\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n    \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/hover-card'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\n  let open = $state(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (open = !open)}\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root bind:open\u003e\n    \u003cp\u003e\n      Liked by\n      \u003cHoverCard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        {#snippet asChild(props)}\n          \u003ca href=\"#profile\" {...props()}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e\n      and 3 others\n    \u003c/p\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Arrow class={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip class={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cimg class={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cp class={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the hover card is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useHoverCard` hook. This\nway you can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard, useHoverCard } from '@ark-ui/react/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const hoverCard = useHoverCard()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eOpen: {String(hoverCard.open)}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.RootProvider value={hoverCard}\u003e\n        \u003cp\u003e\n          Liked by{' '}\n          \u003cHoverCard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} asChild\u003e\n            \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e{' '}\n          and 3 others\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cHoverCard.Arrow className={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n                \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip className={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n              \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.Body}\u003e\n                \u003cimg className={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n                \u003cdiv\u003e\n                  \u003cp className={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                  \u003cp className={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cp className={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard, useHoverCard } from '@ark-ui/solid/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const hoverCard = useHoverCard()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eOpen: {String(hoverCard().open)}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.RootProvider value={hoverCard}\u003e\n        \u003cp\u003e\n          Liked by{' '}\n          \u003cHoverCard.Trigger\n            class={styles.Trigger}\n            asChild={(props) =\u003e (\n              \u003ca href=\"#profile\" {...props()}\u003e\n                @sarah_chen\n              \u003c/a\u003e\n            )}\n          /\u003e{' '}\n          and 3 others\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cHoverCard.Arrow class={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n                \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip class={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n              \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n                \u003cimg class={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n                \u003cdiv\u003e\n                  \u003cp class={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                  \u003cp class={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003cp class={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { HoverCard, useHoverCard } from '@ark-ui/vue/hover-card'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nconst hoverCard = useHoverCard()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003eOpen: {{ String(hoverCard.open) }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cHoverCard.RootProvider :value=\"hoverCard\"\u003e\n      \u003cp\u003e\n        Liked by\n        \u003cHoverCard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" as-child\u003e\n          \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e\n        and 3 others\n      \u003c/p\u003e\n      \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.Arrow :class=\"styles.Arrow\"\u003e\n              \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip :class=\"styles.ArrowTip\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n            \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Body\"\u003e\n              \u003cimg :class=\"styles.Avatar\" src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n              \u003cdiv\u003e\n                \u003cp :class=\"styles.Name\"\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n                \u003cp :class=\"styles.Username\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cp :class=\"styles.Bio\"\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n    \u003c/HoverCard.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { HoverCard, useHoverCard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/hover-card'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const hoverCard = useHoverCard({ id })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003eOpen: {String(hoverCard().open)}\u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003cHoverCard.RootProvider value={hoverCard}\u003e\n    \u003cp\u003e\n      Liked by\n      \u003cHoverCard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        {#snippet asChild(props)}\n          \u003ca href=\"#profile\" {...props()}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e\n      and 3 others\n    \u003c/p\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Arrow class={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip class={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cimg class={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cp class={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/HoverCard.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Delay\n\nControl the open and close delay of the hover card using the `openDelay` and `closeDelay` props:\n\n**Example: delay**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/react/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const Delay = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root openDelay={200} closeDelay={500}\u003e\n    \u003cp\u003e\n      Liked by{' '}\n      \u003cHoverCard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} asChild\u003e\n        \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e{' '}\n      and 3 others\n    \u003c/p\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Arrow className={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip className={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cimg className={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cp className={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/solid/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const Delay = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root openDelay={200} closeDelay={500}\u003e\n    \u003cp\u003e\n      Liked by{' '}\n      \u003cHoverCard.Trigger\n        class={styles.Trigger}\n        asChild={(props) =\u003e (\n          \u003ca href=\"#profile\" {...props()}\u003e\n            @sarah_chen\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cimg class={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cp class={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/vue/hover-card'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root :open-delay=\"200\" :close-delay=\"500\"\u003e\n    \u003cp\u003e\n      Liked by\n \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Positioning\n\nThe `HoverCard` component can be customized in its placement and distance from the trigger element through the\n`positioning` prop:\n\n**Example: positioning**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/react/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const Positioning = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root positioning={{ placement: 'right', gutter: 12 }}\u003e\n    \u003cp\u003e\n      Liked by{' '}\n      \u003cHoverCard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} asChild\u003e\n        \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/a\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e{' '}\n      and 3 others\n    \u003c/p\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Arrow className={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip className={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cimg className={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cp className={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/solid/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from React\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/react/hover-card'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root\u003e\n    \u003cHoverCard.Context\u003e\n      {(context) =\u003e (\n        \u003cp\u003e\n          Liked by{' '}\n          \u003cHoverCard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} asChild\u003e\n            \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e@sarah_chen {context.open ? \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e : \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e}\u003c/a\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Trigger\u003e{' '}\n          and 3 others\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/HoverCard.Context\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Arrow className={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip className={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cimg className={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cp className={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/solid/hover-card'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root\u003e\n    \u003cHoverCard.Context\u003e\n      {(context) =\u003e (\n        \u003cp\u003e\n          Liked by{' '}\n          \u003cHoverCard.Trigger\n            class={styles.Trigger}\n            asChild={(props) =\u003e (\n              \u003ca href=\"#profile\" {...props()}\u003e\n                @sarah_chen {context().open ? \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e : \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e}\n              \u003c/a\u003e\n            )}\n          /\u003e{' '}\n          and 3 others\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/HoverCard.Context\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cHoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cHoverCard.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cHoverCard.Arrow class={styles.Arrow}\u003e\n            \u003cHoverCard.ArrowTip class={styles.ArrowTip} /\u003e\n          \u003c/HoverCard.Arrow\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cimg class={styles.Avatar} src=\"https://i.pravatar.cc/300?u=sarah\" alt=\"Sarah Chen\" /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Name}\u003eSarah Chen\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Username}\u003e@sarah_chen\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003cp class={styles.Bio}\u003eDesign Engineer at Acme Inc.\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/HoverCard.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/HoverCard.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/HoverCard.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { HoverCard } from '@ark-ui/vue/hover-card'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/hover-card.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cHoverCard.Root\u003e\n    \u003cHoverCard.Context v-slot=\"context\"\u003e\n      \u003cp\u003e\n        Liked by\n        \u003cHoverCard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" as-child\u003e\n          \u003ca href=\"#profile\"\u003e\n API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `closeDelay` | `number` | No | The duration from when the mouse leaves the trigger or content until the hover card closes. |\n| `defaultOpen` | `boolean` | No | The initial open state of the hover card when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the open state of the hover card. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the hover card is disabled |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ trigger: string; content: string; positioner: string; arrow: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the popover. Useful for composition. |\n| `immediate` | `boolean` | No | Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `onExitComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Function called when the animation ends in the closed state |\n| `onFocusOutside` | `(event: FocusOutsideEvent) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the focus is moved outside the component |\n| `onInteractOutside` | `(event: InteractOutsideEvent) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when an interaction happens outside the component |\n| `onOpenChange` | `(details: OpenChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the hover card opens or closes. |\n| `onPointerDownOutside` | `(event: PointerDownOutsideEvent) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the pointer is pressed down outside the component |\n| `open` | `boolean` | No | The controlled open state of the hover card |\n| `openDelay` | `number` | No | The duration from when the mouse enters the trigger until the hover card opens. |\n| `positioning` | `PositioningOptions` | No | The user provided options used to position the popover content |\n| `present` | `boolean` | No | Whether the node is present (controlled by the user) |\n| `skipAnimationOnMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow the initial presence animation. |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**Arrow Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Arrow CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--arrow-size` | The size of the arrow |\n| `--arrow-size-half` | Half the size of the arrow |\n| `--arrow-background` | Use this variable to style the arrow background |\n| `--arrow-offset` | The offset position of the arrow |\n\n\n**ArrowTip Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default
